# 大学英语四级考试 (CET-4) 词汇表

## College English Test Band 4 - Complete Vocabulary List

**总词数: 4526** | **Source:** 全国大学英语四、六级考试大纲 (2016修订版)

---


## A

### 1. a

- **词性**: art
- **中**: 一(个)；每一(个)

### 2. abandon [əˈbændən]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 丢弃；放弃，抛弃

### 3. ability [əˈbiliti]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 能力；能耐，本领
- **英**: the quality of having the means or skills to do something

### 4. able [ˈeibl]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 有能力的；出色的
- **英**: having the necessary means or skill to do something

### 5. abnormal [æbˈnɔːməl]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 不正常的；变态的
- **英**: not typical or usual or regular

### 6. aboard [əˈbɔːd]

- **词性**: ad
- **中**: 在船(车)上；上船
- **英**: on a ship, train, plane or other vehicle

### 7. about [ˈəbaut]

- **词性**: prep
- **中**: 关于；在…周围

### 8. above [əˈbʌv]

- **词性**: prep
- **中**: 在…上面；高于

### 9. abroad [əˈbrɔːd]

- **词性**: ad
- **中**: (在)国外；到处
- **英**: to or in a foreign country

### 10. absence [ˈæbsəns]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 缺席，不在场；缺乏
- **英**: the state of being not present

### 11. absent [ˈæbsənt]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 不在场的；缺乏的
- **英**: not being in a specified place

### 12. absolute [ˈæbsəluːt]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 绝对的；纯粹的
- **英**: perfect or complete or pure

### 13. absolutely [ˈæbsəluːtli]

- **词性**: ad
- **中**: 完全地；绝对地
- **英**: totally and definitely; without question

### 14. absorb [əbˈsɔːb]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 吸收；使专心
- **英**: take in a liquid

### 15. abstract [ˈæbstrækt]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 抽象的 n.摘要
- **英**: existing only in the mind

### 16. abundant [əˈbʌndənt]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 丰富的；大量的

### 17. abuse [əˈbjuːz]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 滥用；虐待 n.滥用
- **英**: cruel or inhumane treatment

### 18. academic [ˌækəˈdemik]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 学院的；学术的

### 19. academy [əˈkædəmi]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 私立中学；专科院校

### 20. accelerate [ækˈseləreit]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: (使)加快；促进
- **英**: move faster

### 21. acceleration [ækˌseləˈrei∫ən]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 加速(度)

### 22. accent [ˈæksənt]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 口音，腔调；重音

### 23. accept [əkˈsept]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: vi.接受；同意
- **英**: receive willingly something given or offered

### 24. acceptable [əkˈseptəbl]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 可接受/合意的
- **英**: worthy of approval or satisfactory

### 25. acceptance [əkˈseptəns]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 接受，验收；承认
- **英**: the state of being satisfactory

### 26. access [ˈækses]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 接近；通道，入口
- **英**: the right to enter

### 27. accessory [ækˈsesəri]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 同谋，从犯；附件

### 28. accident [ˈæksidənt]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 意外的；事故
- **英**: an unfortunate mishap

### 29. accidental [ˌæksiˈdentl]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 偶然的；非本质的
- **英**: happening by chance or unexpectedly or unintentionally

### 30. accommodate [əˈkɔmədeit]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 容纳;供应,供给
- **英**: have room for; hold without crowding

### 31. accommodation [əˌkɔməˈdei∫ən]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 招待设备；预定铺位
- **英**: making or becoming suitable; adjusting to circumstances

### 32. accompany [əˈkʌmpəni]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 陪伴，陪同；伴随
- **英**: go or travel along with

### 33. accomplish [əˈkɔmpli∫]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 达到(目的)；完成
- **英**: achieve with effort

### 34. accord [əˈkɔːd]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 使一致；给予
- **英**: concurrence of opinion

### 35. accordance [əˈkɔːdəns]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 一致；和谐；授予
- **英**: concurrence or agreement of opinion

### 36. accordingly [əˈkɔːdiŋli]

- **词性**: ad
- **中**: 因此，所以；照着
- **英**: in agreement with

### 37. account [əˈkaunt]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 记述；解释；帐目
- **英**: a record or narrative description of past events

### 38. accumulate [əˈkjuːmjuleit]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 积累 vi.堆积

### 39. accuracy [ˈækjurəsi]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 准确(性)；准确度
- **英**: the quality of being near to the true value

### 40. accurate [ˈækjurit]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 准确的，正确无误的
- **英**: characterized by perfect conformity to fact or truth

### 41. accuse [əˈkjuːz]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 指责；归咎于
- **英**: blame for; make a claim of wrongdoing or misbehavior against

### 42. accustom [əˈkʌstəm]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 使习惯

### 43. accustomed [əˈkʌstəmd]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 惯常的；习惯的
- **英**: commonly used or practiced; usual

### 44. ache [eik]

- **词性**: vi
- **中**: 痛；想念 n.疼痛
- **英**: a dull persistent (usually moderately intense) pain

### 45. achieve [əˈt∫iːv]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 完成，实现；达到
- **英**: gain with effort

### 46. achievement [əˈt∫iːvmənt]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 完成；成就/绩
- **英**: the action of accomplishing something

### 47. acid [ˈæsid]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 酸；酸的，酸性的

### 48. acquaintance [əˈkweintəns]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 认识;了解;熟人
- **英**: personal knowledge or information about someone or something

### 49. acquire [əˈkwaiə]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 取得；获得；学到
- **英**: come into the possession of something concrete or abstract

### 50. acre [ˈeikə]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 英亩(=6.07 亩)

### 51. across [əˈkrɔs]

- **词性**: prep
- **中**: 横过；在…对面
- **英**: to the opposite side

### 52. act [ækt]

- **词性**: vi
- **中**: 行动；见效 n.行为
- **英**: behave in a certain manner

### 53. action [ˈæk∫ən]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 行动；作用；功能
- **英**: something done (usually as opposed to something said)

### 54. active [ˈæktiv]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 活跃的；积极的
- **英**: characterized by energetic movement

### 55. activity [ækˈtiviti]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 活动；活力；行动
- **英**: any specific behavior

### 56. actor [ˈæktə]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 男演员；演剧的人
- **英**: a performer in theater, television, or film

### 57. actress [ˈæktris]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 女演员
- **英**: a female actor

### 58. actual [ˈæktjuəl]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 实际的；现行的
- **英**: existing in fact

### 59. actually [ˈækt∫uəli]

- **词性**: ad
- **中**: 实际上；竟然
- **英**: in fact

### 60. acute [əˈkjuːt]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 尖的，锐的；敏锐的

### 61. ad [æd]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 广告

### 62. adapt [əˈdæpt]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 使适应；改编
- **英**: make fit for, or change to suit a new purpose

### 63. add [æd]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 添加，附加，掺加
- **英**: join or combine or unite with others

### 64. addition [əˈdi∫ən]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 加，加法；附加物
- **英**: the arithmetic operation of summing

### 65. additional [əˈdi∫ənl]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 附加的，追加的
- **英**: further or extra

### 66. address [əˈdres]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 地址；演说；谈吐

### 67. adequate [ˈædikwit]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 足够的；可以胜任的
- **英**: having the requisite qualities or resources to meet a task

### 68. adjective [ˈædʒiktiv]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 形容词 a.形容词的

### 69. adjust [əˈdʒʌst]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 调整，调节；校正
- **英**: alter or regulate so as to conform to a standard

### 70. administration [ədminisˈtrei∫ən]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 管理；管理部门
- **英**: the act of governing or exercising authority

### 71. admire [ədˈmaiə]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 钦佩，羡慕，赞赏

### 72. admission [ədˈmi∫ən]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 允许进入；承认
- **英**: the act of letting someone enter

### 73. admit [ədˈmit]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 承认；准许…进入
- **英**: declare to be true or accept the reality of

### 74. adopt [əˈdɔpt]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 收养；采用；采取
- **英**: take into one&#039;s family

### 75. adult [ˈædʌlt]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 成年人 a.成年的
- **英**: a fully developed person from maturity onward

### 76. advance [ədˈvɑːns]

- **词性**: vi
- **中**: 前进；提高 n.进展
- **英**: move forward

### 77. advanced [ədˈvɑːnst]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 先进的；高级的
- **英**: situated ahead or going before

### 78. advantage [ədˈvɑːntidʒ]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 优点，优势；好处
- **英**: the quality of having a superior or more favorable position

### 79. adventure [ədˈvent∫ə]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 冒险；惊险活动
- **英**: a wild and exciting undertaking

### 80. adverb [ˈædvəːb]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 副词
- **英**: a word that modifies something other than a noun

### 81. advertisement [ədˈvəːtismənt]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 广告；公告；登广告
- **英**: a public promotion of some product or service

### 82. advice [ədˈvais]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 劝告；忠告；意见
- **英**: a proposal for an appropriate course of action

### 83. advisable [ədˈvaizəbl]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 明智的；可取的
- **英**: worthy of being recommended or suggested; prudent or wise

### 84. advise [ədˈvaiz]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 劝告；建议；通知
- **英**: give advice to

### 85. aeroplane [ˈeərəplein]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 飞机
- **英**: an aircraft that has a fixed wing and is powered by propellers or jets

### 86. affair [əˈfeə]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 事情，事件；事务

### 87. affect [əˈfekt]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 影响；感动
- **英**: have an influence upon

### 88. affection [əˈfek∫ən]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 慈爱，爱；爱慕
- **英**: a positive feeling of liking

### 89. afford [əˈfɔːd]

- **词性**: vt
- **中**: 担负得起…；提供

### 90. afraid [əˈfreid]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 害怕的；担心的

### 91. africa [ˈæfrikə]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 非洲

### 92. african [ˈæfrikən]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 非洲的 n.非洲人

### 93. after [ˈɑːftə]

- **词性**: prep
- **中**: 在…以后；次于

### 94. afternoon [ˈɑːftəˈnuːn]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 下午，午后

### 95. afterward [ˈɑːftəwəd]

- **词性**: ad
- **中**: 后来，以后

- **词性**: ad
- **中**: 又一次；而且

- **中**: 倚在；逆，对着

### 98. age [eidʒ]

- **词性**: n
- **中**: 年龄；时代 vt.变老
- **英**: how long something has existed

- **英**: the state of being in action or exerting power

- **中**: 代理人，代理商
- **英**: a representative who acts on behalf of others

### 101. aggressive [əˈgresiv]

- **词性**: a
- **中**: 侵略的；好斗的
- **英**: characteristic of an enemy or one eager to fight

- **英**: consent or assent to a condition

- **中**: 动物，兽 a.动物的

### 157. ankle [ˈæŋkl]
